\subsection{Macro Definition Documentation}
\hypertarget{tox_8h_a3a8d42ad8b2803ba6d69e88aac567113}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E}}
\index{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E~({\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E} + sizeof(uint32\+\_\+t) + sizeof(uint16\+\_\+t))}}\label{tox_8h_a3a8d42ad8b2803ba6d69e88aac567113}
The size of a Tox address in bytes. Tox addresses are in the format \mbox{[}Public Key (T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E bytes)\mbox{]}\mbox{[}nospam (4 bytes)\mbox{]}\mbox{[}checksum (2 bytes)\mbox{]}.

The checksum is computed over the Public Key and the nospam value. The first byte is an X\+O\+R of all the even bytes (0, 2, 4, ...), the second byte is an X\+O\+R of all the odd bytes (1, 3, 5, ...) of the Public Key and nospam. 

Definition at line 235 of file tox.\+h.



Referenced by fraddr\+\_\+to\+\_\+str(), get\+\_\+id(), main(), print\+\_\+friendlist(), and S\+T\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T().

\hypertarget{tox_8h_af80a3c50ad465fbd07df3d5fc144aa1b}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+D@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+D}}
\index{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+D@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+D}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+D}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+D}}\label{tox_8h_af80a3c50ad465fbd07df3d5fc144aa1b}
Events are handled by callbacks. One callback can be registered per event. All events have a callback function type named {\ttfamily tox\+\_\+\{event\}\+\_\+cb} and a function to register it named {\ttfamily tox\+\_\+callback\+\_\+\{event\}}. Passing a N\+U\+L\+L callback will result in no callback being registered for that event. Only one callback per event can be registered, so if a client needs multiple event listeners, it needs to implement the dispatch functionality itself.

It is possible to run multiple concurrent threads with a Tox instance for each thread. It is also possible to run all Tox instances in the same thread. A common way to run Tox (multiple or single instance) is to have one thread running a simple tox\+\_\+iterate loop, sleeping for tox\+\_\+iteration\+\_\+interval milliseconds on each iteration.

If you want to access a single Tox instance from multiple threads, access to the instance must be synchronised. While multiple threads can concurrently access multiple different Tox instances, no more than one A\+P\+I function can operate on a single instance at any given time.

Functions that write to variable length byte arrays will always have a size function associated with them. The result of this size function is only valid until another mutating function (one that takes a pointer to non-\/const Tox) is called. Thus, clients must ensure that no other thread calls a mutating function between the call to the size function and the call to the retrieval function.

E.\+g. to get the current nickname, one would write


\begin{DoxyCode}
1 size\_t length = tox\_self\_get\_name\_size(tox);
2 uint8\_t *name = malloc(length);
3 if (!name) abort();
4 tox\_self\_get\_name(tox, name);
\end{DoxyCode}


If any other thread calls tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+set\+\_\+name while this thread is allocating memory, the length may have become invalid, and the call to tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+name may cause undefined behaviour. The Tox instance type. All the state associated with a connection is held within the instance. Multiple instances can exist and operate concurrently. The maximum number of Tox instances that can exist on a single network device is limited. Note that this is not just a per-\/process limit, since the limiting factor is the number of usable ports on a device.

\subsubsection[{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef enum {\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O}  {\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O}}}\label{tox_8h_a099a96e94825c1069a4da99291a833bf}
Common error codes for all functions that set a piece of user-\/visible client information. \hypertarget{tox_8h_a81c5caff41c6f8732c29da53efe9c287}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G}}
\index{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef enum {\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G}  {\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+I\+N\+G}}}\label{tox_8h_a81c5caff41c6f8732c29da53efe9c287}
\hypertarget{tox_8h_a38d6f55204227c8f22ddf8fbb67fa7b2}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request\+\_\+cb@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request\+\_\+cb}}
\index{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request\+\_\+cb@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request\+\_\+cb}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request\+\_\+cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request\+\_\+cb({\bf Tox} $\ast$tox, uint32\+\_\+t {\bf friend\+\_\+number}, uint32\+\_\+t file\+\_\+number, uint64\+\_\+t position, size\+\_\+t length, void $\ast$user\+\_\+data)}}\label{tox_8h_a38d6f55204227c8f22ddf8fbb67fa7b2}
If the length parameter is 0, the file transfer is finished, and the client's resources associated with the file number should be released. After a call with zero length, the file number can be reused for future file transfers.

If the requested position is not equal to the client's idea of the current file or stream position, it will need to seek. In case of read-\/once streams, the client should keep the last read chunk so that a seek back can be supported. A seek-\/back only ever needs to read from the last requested chunk. This happens when a chunk was requested, but the send failed. A seek-\/back request can occur an arbitrary number of times for any given chunk.

In response to receiving this callback, the client should call the function {\ttfamily tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk} with the requested chunk. If the number of bytes sent through that function is zero, the file transfer is assumed complete. A client must send the full length of data requested with this callback.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em friend\+\_\+number} & The friend number of the receiving friend for this file. \\
\hline
{\em file\+\_\+number} & The file transfer identifier returned by tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send. \\
\hline
{\em position} & The file or stream position from which to continue reading. \\
\hline
{\em length} & The number of bytes requested for the current chunk. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a643ef568a8ddd7b81511dcebc9f11518}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L}}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a2433b6cc976ef6d1bbe173baf4b2bb7f}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+cb@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+cb}}
\index{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+cb@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+cb}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+cb({\bf Tox} $\ast$tox, uint32\+\_\+t {\bf friend\+\_\+number}, uint32\+\_\+t file\+\_\+number, uint32\+\_\+t kind, uint64\+\_\+t {\bf file\+\_\+size}, const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$filename, size\+\_\+t filename\+\_\+length, void $\ast$user\+\_\+data)}}\label{tox_8h_a2433b6cc976ef6d1bbe173baf4b2bb7f}
The client should acquire resources to be associated with the file transfer. Incoming file transfers start in the P\+A\+U\+S\+E\+D state. After this callback returns, a transfer can be rejected by sending a T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+N\+C\+E\+L control command before any other control commands. It can be accepted by sending T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+U\+M\+E.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em friend\+\_\+number} & The friend number of the friend who is sending the file transfer request. \\
\hline
{\em file\+\_\+number} & The friend-\/specific file number the data received is associated with. \\
\hline
{\em kind} & The meaning of the file to be sent. \\
\hline
{\em file\+\_\+size} & Size in bytes of the file the client wants to send, U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X if unknown or streaming. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & Name of the file. Does not need to be the actual name. This name will be sent along with the file send request. \\
\hline
{\em filename\+\_\+length} & Size in bytes of the filename. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Definition at line 2071 of file tox.\+h.

\hypertarget{tox_8h_ac17866d2bb797a329f810b973157e0ae}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+cb@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+cb}}
\index{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+cb@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+cb}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+recv\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+cb({\bf Tox} $\ast$tox, uint32\+\_\+t {\bf friend\+\_\+number}, uint32\+\_\+t file\+\_\+number, uint64\+\_\+t position, const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$data, size\+\_\+t length, void $\ast$user\+\_\+data)}}\label{tox_8h_ac17866d2bb797a329f810b973157e0ae}
When length is 0, the transfer is finished and the client should release the resources it acquired for the transfer. After a call with length = 0, the file number can be reused for new file transfers.

If position is equal to file\+\_\+size (received in the file\+\_\+receive callback) when the transfer finishes, the file was received completely. Otherwise, if file\+\_\+size was U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X, streaming ended successfully when length is 0.

\hline
{\em data} & A byte array containing the received chunk. \\
\hline
{\em length} & The length of the received chunk. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a8fddeeee28ccfa73c93f5c6bb807ff93a70959d02490e1b658c7d7daf262869a0}{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+K\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A}\label{tox_8h_a8fddeeee28ccfa73c93f5c6bb807ff93a70959d02490e1b658c7d7daf262869a0}
}]Arbitrary file data. Clients can choose to handle it based on the file name or magic or any other way they choose. \index{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+K\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+V\+A\+T\+A\+R@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+K\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+V\+A\+T\+A\+R}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+K\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+V\+A\+T\+A\+R@{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+K\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+V\+A\+T\+A\+R}}\item[{\em 
\hypertarget{tox_8h_a8fddeeee28ccfa73c93f5c6bb807ff93a7ce277151c9a76736c40a50325a2d1b2}{T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+K\+I\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+V\+A\+T\+A\+R}\label{tox_8h_a8fddeeee28ccfa73c93f5c6bb807ff93a7ce277151c9a76736c40a50325a2d1b2}
}]Avatar file\+\_\+id. This consists of tox\+\_\+hash(image). Avatar data. This consists of the image data.

Avatars can be sent at any time the client wishes. Generally, a client will send the avatar to a friend when that friend comes online, and to all friends when the avatar changed. A client can save some traffic by remembering which friend received the updated avatar already and only send it if the friend has an out of date avatar.

Clients who receive avatar send requests can reject it (by sending T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+N\+C\+E\+L before any other controls), or accept it (by sending T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+U\+M\+E). The file\+\_\+id of length T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+H\+A\+S\+H\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H bytes (same length as T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+D\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H) will contain the hash. A client can compare this hash with a saved hash and send T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+N\+C\+E\+L to terminate the avatar transfer if it matches.

When file\+\_\+size is set to 0 in the transfer request it means that the client has no avatar. \end{description}
\end{Desc}

\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{tox_8h_ae858a499d7f8e2e5cbf5533afbd20537}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+add\+\_\+tcp\+\_\+relay@{tox\+\_\+add\+\_\+tcp\+\_\+relay}}
\index{tox\+\_\+add\+\_\+tcp\+\_\+relay@{tox\+\_\+add\+\_\+tcp\+\_\+relay}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+add\+\_\+tcp\+\_\+relay}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool tox\+\_\+add\+\_\+tcp\+\_\+relay (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{address, }
\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{port, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{public\+\_\+key, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+T\+S\+T\+R\+A\+P} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_ae858a499d7f8e2e5cbf5533afbd20537}
Adds additional host\+:port pair as T\+C\+P relay.

This function can be used to initiate T\+C\+P connections to different ports on the same bootstrap node, or to add T\+C\+P relays without using them as bootstrap nodes.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em address} & The hostname or \hyperlink{struct_i_p}{I\+P} address (I\+Pv4 or I\+Pv6) of the T\+C\+P relay. \\
\hline
{\em port} & The port on the host on which the T\+C\+P relay is listening. \\
\hline
{\em public\+\_\+key} & The long term public key of the T\+C\+P relay (T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E bytes). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true on success. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_ae7e49c1e9e6c3a0f9e55bfcb78044c1e}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+bootstrap@{tox\+\_\+bootstrap}}
\index{tox\+\_\+bootstrap@{tox\+\_\+bootstrap}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+bootstrap}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool tox\+\_\+bootstrap (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{address, }
\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{port, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{public\+\_\+key, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+T\+S\+T\+R\+A\+P} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_ae7e49c1e9e6c3a0f9e55bfcb78044c1e}
Sends a \char`\"{}get nodes\char`\"{} request to the given bootstrap node with \hyperlink{struct_i_p}{I\+P}, port, and public key to setup connections.

This function will attempt to connect to the node using U\+D\+P. You must use this function even if \hyperlink{struct_tox___options_a35c23f2b9cd2468e2a256ca93a21d5d5}{Tox\+\_\+\+Options.\+udp\+\_\+enabled} was set to false.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em address} & The hostname or \hyperlink{struct_i_p}{I\+P} address (I\+Pv4 or I\+Pv6) of the node. \\
\hline
{\em port} & The port on the host on which the bootstrap Tox instance is listening. \\
\hline
{\em public\+\_\+key} & The long term public key of the bootstrap node (T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E bytes). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true on success. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+callback\+\_\+self\+\_\+connection\+\_\+status}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void tox\+\_\+callback\+\_\+self\+\_\+connection\+\_\+status (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{{\bf tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+connection\+\_\+status\+\_\+cb} $\ast$}]{callback, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{user\+\_\+data}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a198a638f434f814c216de71ad394dab2}
Set the callback for the {\ttfamily self\+\_\+connection\+\_\+status} event. Pass N\+U\+L\+L to unset.

This event is triggered whenever there is a change in the \hyperlink{struct_d_h_t}{D\+H\+T} connection state. When disconnected, a client may choose to call tox\+\_\+bootstrap again, to reconnect to the \hyperlink{struct_d_h_t}{D\+H\+T}. Note that this state may frequently change for short amounts of time. Clients should therefore not immediately bootstrap on receiving a disconnect.

T\+O\+D\+O\+: how long should a client wait before bootstrapping again?

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a57990fd242dca24aa7e1f29f5fa56be7}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send}}
\index{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{friend\+\_\+number, }
\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{kind, }
\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{file\+\_\+size, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{file\+\_\+id, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{filename, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{filename\+\_\+length, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+D} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a57990fd242dca24aa7e1f29f5fa56be7}
Send a file transmission request.

Maximum filename length is T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H bytes. The filename should generally just be a file name, not a path with directory names.

If a non-\/\+U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X file size is provided, it can be used by both sides to determine the sending progress. File size can be set to U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X for streaming data of unknown size.

File transmission occurs in chunks, which are requested through the {\ttfamily file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request} event.

When a friend goes offline, all file transfers associated with the friend are purged from core.

If the file contents change during a transfer, the behaviour is unspecified in general. What will actually happen depends on the mode in which the file was modified and how the client determines the file size.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the file size was increased
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item and sending mode was streaming (file\+\_\+size = U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X), the behaviour will be as expected.
\item and sending mode was file (file\+\_\+size != U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X), the file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request callback will receive length = 0 when Core thinks the file transfer has finished. If the client remembers the file size as it was when sending the request, it will terminate the transfer normally. If the client re-\/reads the size, it will think the friend cancelled the transfer.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item If the file size was decreased
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item and sending mode was streaming, the behaviour is as expected.
\item and sending mode was file, the callback will return 0 at the new (earlier) end-\/of-\/file, signalling to the friend that the transfer was cancelled.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item If the file contents were modified
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item at a position before the current read, the two files (local and remote) will differ after the transfer terminates.
\item at a position after the current read, the file transfer will succeed as expected.
\item In either case, both sides will regard the transfer as complete and successful.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em friend\+\_\+number} & The friend number of the friend the file send request should be sent to. \\
\hline
{\em kind} & The meaning of the file to be sent. \\
\hline
{\em file\+\_\+size} & Size in bytes of the file the client wants to send, U\+I\+N\+T64\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X if unknown or streaming. \\
\hline
{\em file\+\_\+id} & A file identifier of length T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+D\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H that can be used to uniquely identify file transfers across core restarts. If N\+U\+L\+L, a random one will be generated by core. It can then be obtained by using \hyperlink{tox_8h_a93de44f83bd544d48d279d6c52ee48cc}{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+get\+\_\+file\+\_\+id()}. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & Name of the file. Does not need to be the actual name. This name will be sent along with the file send request. \\
\hline
{\em filename\+\_\+length} & Size in bytes of the filename.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A file number used as an identifier in subsequent callbacks. This number is per friend. File numbers are reused after a transfer terminates. On failure, this function returns U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X. Any pattern in file numbers should not be relied on. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line 1034 of file tox.\+c.

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a7653dd0bbf8bda8e18d211277f3e7577}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk}}
\index{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk@{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send\+\_\+chunk (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{friend\+\_\+number, }
\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{file\+\_\+number, }
\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{position, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{data, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+C\+H\+U\+N\+K} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a7653dd0bbf8bda8e18d211277f3e7577}
Send a chunk of file data to a friend.

This function is called in response to the {\ttfamily file\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+request} callback. The length parameter should be equal to the one received though the callback. If it is zero, the transfer is assumed complete. For files with known size, Core will know that the transfer is complete after the last byte has been received, so it is not necessary (though not harmful) to send a zero-\/length chunk to terminate. For streams, core will know that the transfer is finished if a chunk with length less than the length requested in the callback is sent.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em friend\+\_\+number} & The friend number of the receiving friend for this file. \\
\hline
{\em file\+\_\+number} & The file transfer identifier returned by tox\+\_\+file\+\_\+send. \\
\hline
{\em position} & The file or stream position from which to continue reading. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true on success. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_aa921c439baad10c03f8d93fda753b0b8}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add@{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add}}
\index{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add@{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{address, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{message, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_aa921c439baad10c03f8d93fda753b0b8}
Add a friend to the friend list and send a friend request.

A friend request message must be at least 1 byte long and at most T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H.

\hyperlink{struct_friend}{Friend} numbers are unique identifiers used in all functions that operate on friends. Once added, a friend number is stable for the lifetime of the Tox object. After saving the state and reloading it, the friend numbers may not be the same as before. Deleting a friend creates a gap in the friend number set, which is filled by the next adding of a friend. Any pattern in friend numbers should not be relied on.

If more than I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X friends are added, this function causes undefined behaviour.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em address} & The address of the friend (returned by tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+address of the friend you wish to add) it must be T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E bytes. \\
\hline
{\em message} & The message that will be sent along with the friend request. \\
\hline
{\em length} & The length of the data byte array.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the friend number on success, U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line 557 of file tox.\+c.

\hypertarget{tox_8h_ad499c853b628d04dd0f3c6ef5a14ebe4}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add\+\_\+norequest@{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add\+\_\+norequest}}
\index{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add\+\_\+norequest@{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add\+\_\+norequest}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add\+\_\+norequest}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add\+\_\+norequest (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{public\+\_\+key, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_ad499c853b628d04dd0f3c6ef5a14ebe4}
Add a friend without sending a friend request.

This function is used to add a friend in response to a friend request. If the client receives a friend request, it can be reasonably sure that the other client added this client as a friend, eliminating the need for a friend request.

This function is also useful in a situation where both instances are controlled by the same entity, so that this entity can perform the mutual friend adding. In this case, there is no need for a friend request, either.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em public\+\_\+key} & A byte array of length T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E containing the Public Key (not the Address) of the friend to add.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the friend number on success, U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{tox_8h_aa921c439baad10c03f8d93fda753b0b8}{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+add} \hyperlink{toxav__many__test_8c_a8799beff27c0e5459ef50f9ca1efe92c}{for} a more detailed description of friend numbers. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Remove a friend from the friend list.

This does not notify the friend of their deletion. After calling this function, this client will appear offline to the friend and no communication can occur between the two.

Write the status message of the friend designated by the given friend number to a byte array.

Call tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+get\+\_\+status\+\_\+message\+\_\+size to determine the allocation size for the {\ttfamily status\+\_\+name} parameter.

The data written to {\ttfamily status\+\_\+message} is equal to the data received by the last {\ttfamily friend\+\_\+status\+\_\+message} callback.

\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+lossless\+\_\+packet}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+lossless\+\_\+packet (

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_ac162368b375a58b5d7d4b29584449bdd}
Send a custom lossless packet to a friend.

The first byte of data must be in the range 160-\/191. Maximum length of a custom packet is T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E.

Lossless packet behaviour is comparable to T\+C\+P (reliability, arrive in order) but with packets instead of a stream.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true on success. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+lossy\+\_\+packet}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+lossy\+\_\+packet (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{friend\+\_\+number, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{data, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+E\+T} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a83a51aeda057c82ed1e844962a84fe46}
Send a custom lossy packet to a friend.

The first byte of data must be in the range 200-\/254. Maximum length of a custom packet is T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E.

Lossy packets behave like U\+D\+P packets, meaning they might never reach the other side or might arrive more than once (if someone is messing with the connection) or might arrive in the wrong order.

Unless latency is an issue, it is recommended that you use lossless custom packets instead.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em friend\+\_\+number} & The friend number of the friend this lossy packet should be sent to. \\
\hline
{\em data} & A byte array containing the packet data. \\
\hline
{\em length} & The length of the packet data byte array.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true on success. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a89cd6aedba9fca87bd66a9713dc6b503}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+message@{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+message}}
\index{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+message@{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+message}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+message}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t tox\+\_\+friend\+\_\+send\+\_\+message (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{friend\+\_\+number, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+S\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E}}]{type, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{message, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+R\+I\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+S\+A\+G\+E} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a89cd6aedba9fca87bd66a9713dc6b503}
Send a text chat message to an online friend.

This function creates a chat message packet and pushes it into the send queue.

The message length may not exceed T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+S\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H. Larger messages must be split by the client and sent as separate messages. Other clients can then reassemble the fragments. Messages may not be empty.

The return value of this function is the message I\+D. If a read receipt is received, the triggered {\ttfamily friend\+\_\+read\+\_\+receipt} event will be passed this message I\+D.

Message I\+Ds are unique per friend. The first message I\+D is 0. Message I\+Ds are incremented by 1 each time a message is sent. If U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X messages were sent, the next message I\+D is 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em type} & Message type (normal, action, ...). \\
\hline
{\em friend\+\_\+number} & The friend number of the friend to send the message to. \\
\hline
{\em message} & A non-\/\+N\+U\+L\+L pointer to the first element of a byte array containing the message text. \\
\hline
{\em length} & Length of the message to be sent. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Definition at line 867 of file tox.\+c.

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a755ba12184aab759f9fcd5fa06d09ebc}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+hash@{tox\+\_\+hash}}
\index{tox\+\_\+hash@{tox\+\_\+hash}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+hash}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool tox\+\_\+hash (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{hash, }
\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{data, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a755ba12184aab759f9fcd5fa06d09ebc}
Generates a cryptographic hash of the given data.

This function may be used by clients for any purpose, but is provided primarily for validating cached avatars. This use is highly recommended to avoid unnecessary avatar updates.

If hash is N\+U\+L\+L or data is N\+U\+L\+L while length is not 0 the function returns false, otherwise it returns true.

This function is a wrapper to internal message-\/digest functions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em hash} & A valid memory location the hash data. It must be at least T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+H\+A\+S\+H\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H bytes in size. \\
\hline
{\em data} & Data to be hashed or N\+U\+L\+L. \\
\hline
{\em length} & Size of the data array or 0.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if hash was not N\+U\+L\+L. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item[{{\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a52259e134bfb9396d9fef4fffe94e878}
Releases all resources associated with the Tox instance and disconnects from the network.

After calling this function, the Tox pointer becomes invalid. No other functions can be called, and the pointer value can no longer be read.

\hypertarget{tox_8h_aa0e6afccd06a766b84a0633e259f9165}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+new@{tox\+\_\+new}}
\index{tox\+\_\+new@{tox\+\_\+new}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf Tox}$\ast$ tox\+\_\+new (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const struct {\bf Tox\+\_\+\+Options} $\ast$}]{options, }
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+E\+W} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_aa0e6afccd06a766b84a0633e259f9165}


Creates and initialises a new Tox instance with the options passed. 

This function will bring the instance into a valid state. Running the event loop with a new instance will operate correctly.

If loading failed or succeeded only partially, the new or partially loaded instance is returned and an error code is set.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em options} & An options object as described above. If this parameter is N\+U\+L\+L, the default options are used.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{tox_8h_a649c8740c523fb52272396cb0b70b8dc}{tox\+\_\+iterate} \hyperlink{toxav__many__test_8c_a8799beff27c0e5459ef50f9ca1efe92c}{for} the event loop.
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new Tox instance pointer on success or N\+U\+L\+L on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_ac9b57278d2ca390623624409303ea390}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+default@{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+default}}
\index{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+default@{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+default}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+default}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+default (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf Tox\+\_\+\+Options} $\ast$}]{options}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_ac9b57278d2ca390623624409303ea390}
Initialises a \hyperlink{struct_tox___options}{Tox\+\_\+\+Options} object with the default options.

The result of this function is independent of the original options. All values will be overwritten, no values will be read (so it is permissible to pass an uninitialised object).

If options is N\+U\+L\+L, this function has no effect.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em options} & An options object to be filled with default options. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Referenced by load\+\_\+data(), S\+T\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T(), and tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new().

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a5736fd01eb6129d6f817b780cd4262bb}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new@{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new}}
\index{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new@{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}struct {\bf Tox\+\_\+\+Options}$\ast$ tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+new (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+N\+E\+W} $\ast$}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a5736fd01eb6129d6f817b780cd4262bb}
Allocates a new \hyperlink{struct_tox___options}{Tox\+\_\+\+Options} object and initialises it with the default options. This function can be used to preserve long term A\+B\+I compatibility by giving the responsibility of allocation and deallocation to the Tox library.

Objects returned from this function must be freed using the tox\+\_\+options\+\_\+free function.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new \hyperlink{struct_tox___options}{Tox\+\_\+\+Options} object with default options or N\+U\+L\+L on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+address}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+address (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const {\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{address}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_ab52d4512e58c7ff8f62121beff5c0a49}
Writes the Tox friend address of the client to a byte array. The address is not in human-\/readable format. If a client wants to display the address, formatting is required.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hypertarget{tox_8h_a236f8d39263db221678cfd6513fa3161}{\index{tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}!tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+dht\+\_\+id@{tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+dht\+\_\+id}}
\index{tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+dht\+\_\+id@{tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+dht\+\_\+id}!tox.\+h@{tox.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+dht\+\_\+id}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+dht\+\_\+id (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const {\bf Tox} $\ast$}]{tox, }
\item[{uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{dht\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{tox_8h_a236f8d39263db221678cfd6513fa3161}
Writes the temporary \hyperlink{struct_d_h_t}{D\+H\+T} public key of this instance to a byte array.

This can be used in combination with an externally accessible \hyperlink{struct_i_p}{I\+P} address and the bound port (from tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+udp\+\_\+port) to run a temporary bootstrap node.

Be aware that every time a new instance is created, the \hyperlink{struct_d_h_t}{D\+H\+T} public key changes, meaning this cannot be used to run a permanent bootstrap node.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dht\+\_\+id} & A memory region of at least T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E bytes. If this parameter is N\+U\+L\+L, this function has no effect. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Write the nickname set by tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+set\+\_\+name to a byte array.

If no nickname was set before calling this function, the name is empty, and this function has no effect.

Call tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+name\+\_\+size to find out how much memory to allocate for the result.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

Write the status message set by tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+set\+\_\+status\+\_\+message to a byte array.

If no status message was set before calling this function, the status is empty, and this function has no effect.

Call tox\+\_\+self\+\_\+get\+\_\+status\+\_\+message\+\_\+size to find out how much memory to allocate for the result.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em status} & A valid memory location large enough to hold the status message. If this parameter is N\+U\+L\+L, the function has no effect. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Set the nickname for the Tox client.

Nickname length cannot exceed T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H. If length is 0, the name parameter is ignored (it can be N\+U\+L\+L), and the nickname is set back to empty.

Set the client's status message.

Status message length cannot exceed T\+O\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+S\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N\+G\+T\+H. If length is 0, the status parameter is ignored (it can be N\+U\+L\+L), and the user status is set back to empty.
